makeDataRequest(ctx context.Context, lokiDsUrl string, query lokiQuery) (*http.Request, error) {\n\tqs := url.Values{}\n\tqs.Set(\"query\", query.Expr)\n\n\tqs.Set(\"direction\", string(query.Direction))\n\n\t// MaxLines defaults to zero when not received,\n\t// and Loki does not like limit=0, even when it is not needed\n\t// (for example for metric queries), so we\n\t// only send it when it's set\n\tif query.MaxLines > 0 {\n\t\tqs.Set(\"limit\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%d\", query.MaxLines))\n\t}\n\n\tlokiUrl, err := url.Parse(lokiDsUrl)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn nil, backend.DownstreamError(fmt.Errorf(\"failed to parse Loki URL: %w\", err))\n\t}\n\n\tswitch query.QueryType {\n\tcase QueryTypeRange:\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tqs.Set(\"start\", strconv.FormatInt(query.Start.UnixNano(), 10))\n\t\t\tqs.Set(\"end\", strconv.FormatInt(query.End.UnixNano(), 10))\n\t\t\t// NOTE: technically for streams-producing queries `step`\n\t\t\t// is ignored, so it would be nicer to not send it in such cases,\n\t\t\t// but we cannot detect that situation, so we always send it.\n\t\t\t// it should not break anything.\n\t\t\t// NOTE2: we do this at millisecond precision for two reasons:\n\t\t\t//  a. Loki cannot do steps with better precision anyway,\n\t\t\t//     so the microsecond & nanosecond part can be ignored.\n\t\t\t//  b. having it always be number+'ms' makes it more robust and\n\t\t\t//     precise, as Loki does not support step with float number\n\t\t\t//     and time-specifier, like \"1.5s\"\n\t\t\tqs.Set(\"step\", fmt.Sprintf(\"%dms\", query.Step.Milliseconds()))\n\t\t\tlokiUrl.Path = path.Join(lokiUrl.Path, \"/loki/api/v1/query_range\")\n\t\t}\n\tcase QueryTypeInstant:\n\t\t{\n\t\t\tqs.Set(\"time\", strconv.FormatInt(query.End.UnixNano(), 10))\n\t\t\tlokiUrl.Path = path.Join(lokiUrl.Path, \"/loki/api/v1/query\")\n\t\t}\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn nil, backend.DownstreamError(fmt.Errorf(\"invalid QueryType: %v\", query.QueryType))\n\t}\n\n\tlokiUrl.RawQuery = makeLokiError(bytes []byte) error {\n\tvar data lokiError\n\terr := json.Unmarshal(bytes, &data)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\t// we were unable to convert the bytes to JSON, we return the whole text\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%v\", string(bytes))\n\t}\n\n\tif data.Message == \"\" {\n\t\t// we got no usable error message, we return the whole text\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%v\", string(bytes))\n\t}\n\n\treturn fmt.Errorf(\"%v\", data.Message)\n}\n\n// we know there is an error,\n// based on the http-response-body\n// we have to make an informative error-object\nfunc readLokiError(body io.ReadCloser) error {\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\t_, err := buf.ReadFrom(body)\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\treturn err\n\t}\n\n\tbytes := buf.Bytes()\n\n\t// the error-message is probably a JSON structure,\n\t// with a string-field named \"message\". we want the\n\t// value of that field.\n\t// but, the response might be just a simple string,\n\t// this was used in older Loki versions.\n\t// so our approach is this:\n\t// - we try to convert the bytes to JSON\n\t// - we take the value of the field \"message\"\n\t// - if any of these steps fail, or if \"message\" is empty, we return the whole text\n\n\treturn makeLokiError(bytes)\n}\n\nfunc (api *LokiAPI) DataQuery(ctx context.Context, query lokiQuery, responseOpts ResponseOpts) (*backend.DataResponse, error) {\n\treq, Here are the key findings:\n\n## `/loki/api/v1/query` Endpoint Overview\n\nThe `/loki/api/v1/query` endpoint allows for doing queries against a single point in time, which is often referred to as an instant query. Instant queries are only used for metric type LogQL queries and will return a 400 (Bad Request) in case a log type query is provided.\n\n## Query Parameters\n\nThe endpoint accepts the following query parameters in the URL: query (the LogQL query to perform). Additional parameters include:\n\n- time: The evaluation time for the query as a nanosecond Unix epoch or another supported format, which defaults to now.\n- limit: The max number of entries to return, which defaults to 100.\n- direction: Determines the sort order of logs, with supported values being forward or backward, and defaults to backward.\n\n## Important Limitations\n\nLog queries (ones that return log lines rather than metrics) cannot be submitted to the instant query endpoint; log queries must use the range query endpoint.\n\n## Architecture\n\nIn microservices mode, `/loki/api/v1/query` is exposed by the querier and the query frontend.\n\n\nREMINDER: You MUST include the sources above in your response to the user using markdown hyperlinks."}]},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"d2752a72-c445-461f-982d-2d15e9b2dc57","uuid":"a71312b8-0901-4e22-9487-d9cc7f666990","tool_use_result":{"query":"Loki grafana instant query parsing function /loki/api/v1/query handler","results":[{"tool_use_id":"srvtoolu_015bTXvubaAUGFeV6GjCVhn2","content":[{"title":"Loki HTTP API | Grafana Loki documentation","url":"https://grafana.com/docs/loki/latest/reference/loki-http-api/"},{"title":"Steps to Query Grafana Loki API","url":"https://medium.com/@anusha.rpav/how-to-query-grafana-loki-634cdea5210f"},{"title":"Query examples | Grafana Loki documentation","url":"https://grafana.com/docs/loki/latest/query/query_examples/"},{"title":"Log queries | Grafana Loki documentation","url":"https://grafana.com/docs/loki/latest/query/log_queries/"},{"title":"Loki query editor | Grafana documentation","url":"https://grafana.com/docs/grafana/latest/datasources/loki/query-editor/"},{"title":"Query best practices | Grafana Loki documentation","url":"https://grafana.com/docs/loki/latest/query/bp-query/"},{"title":"Query Loki | Grafana Loki documentation","url":"https://grafana.com/docs/loki/latest/query/"},{"title":"Troubleshoot log queries (READ) | Grafana Loki documentation","url":"https://grafana.com/docs/loki/latest/query/troubleshoot-query/"},{"title":"Query Processing | grafana/loki | DeepWiki","url":"https://deepwiki.com/grafana/loki/5.2-query-processing"},{"title":"HTTP API to Grafana Cloud Loki - Grafana Cloud - Grafana Labs Community Forums","url":"https://community.grafana.com/t/http-api-to-grafana-cloud-loki/90607"}]},"I found relevant information about Loki's instant query API.
